    <script>

        // if getParameterByName function is not defined, define it
        if (typeof getParameterByName === 'undefined') {
            function getParameterByName(name, url) {
                if (!url) url = window.location.href;
                name = name.replace(/[\[\]]/g, "\\$&");
                var regex = new RegExp("[?&]" + name + "(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)"),
                    results = regex.exec(url);
                if (!results) return null;
                if (!results[2]) return '';
                return decodeURIComponent(results[2].replace(/\+/g, " "));
            }
        }

        jQuery(document).ready(function($) {

            // First detect if _GET params are present.
            // We only need utm_source, utm_medium and utm_campaign
            var utm_source = getParameterByName('utm_source');
            var utm_medium = getParameterByName('utm_medium');
            var utm_campaign = getParameterByName('utm_campaign');
            var utm_content = getParameterByName('utm_content');
            var utm_term = getParameterByName('utm_term');

            // Next we will use Cookies.js to set cookies

            // If _GET params are present, set cookies
            if (utm_source) {
                Cookies.set('kela_utm_source', utm_source, { expires: 1, path: '/' });
            }
            if (utm_medium) {
                Cookies.set('kela_utm_medium', utm_medium, { expires: 1, path: '/' });
            }
            if (utm_campaign) {
                Cookies.set('kela_utm_campaign', utm_campaign, { expires: 1, path: '/' });
            }
            if (utm_content) {
                Cookies.set('kela_utm_content', utm_content, { expires: 1, path: '/' });
            }
            if (utm_term) {
                Cookies.set('kela_utm_term', utm_term, { expires: 1, path: '/' });
            }

            // Check if cookies are present
            if (Cookies.get('kela_utm_source')) {
                utm_source = Cookies.get('kela_utm_source');
            }
            if (Cookies.get('kela_utm_medium')) {
                utm_medium = Cookies.get('kela_utm_medium');
            }
            if (Cookies.get('kela_utm_campaign')) {
                utm_campaign = Cookies.get('kela_utm_campaign');
            }
            if (Cookies.get('kela_utm_content')) {
                utm_content = Cookies.get('kela_utm_content');
            }
            if (Cookies.get('kela_utm_term')) {
                utm_term = Cookies.get('kela_utm_term');
            }

            // Wait 4 seconds for the form to load
            setTimeout(function() {
                
                // Find if hidden fields exist, for example: .hs-utm_campaign input
                if ($(".hs-utm_source input").length) {
                    $(".hs-utm_source input").val(utm_source);
                }
                if ($(".hs-utm_medium input").length) {
                    $(".hs-utm_medium input").val(utm_medium);
                }   

                if ($(".hs-utm_campaign input").length) {
                    $(".hs-utm_campaign input").val(utm_campaign);
                }

                if ($(".hs-utm_content input").length) {
                    $(".hs-utm_content input").val(utm_content);
                }

                if ($(".hs-utm_term input").length) {
                    $(".hs-utm_term input").val(utm_term);
                }

                if ($(".gfield--type-text.utm_source input").length) {
                    $(".gfield--type-text.utm_source input").val(utm_source);
                }

                if ($(".gfield--type-text.utm_medium input").length) {
                    $(".gfield--type-text.utm_medium input").val(utm_medium);
                }

                if ($(".gfield--type-text.utm_campaign input").length) {
                    $(".gfield--type-text.utm_campaign input").val(utm_campaign);
                }

                    $(".gfield--type-text.utm_content input").val(utm_content);
                }

                if ($(".gfield--type-text.utm_term input").length) {
                    $(".gfield--type-text.utm_term input").val(utm_term);
                }
                
            }, 4000);
